  2587. # [19:36] <bent> let me see if i can explain simply
  2588. # [19:36] <bent> nsCOMPtr and nsRefPtr are basically just templates that hold a T*
  2589. # [19:37] <bent> nsRefPtr<nsIFoo> and nsRefPtr<Foo> hold two different types, nsIFoo* and Foo*
  2590. # [19:37] <bent> if you want to call a method on Foo that doesn't exist on nsIFoo then you can't do that with a nsIFoo*
  2591. # [19:38] <bent> nsCOMPtr just adds a little bit on top of nsRefPtr
  2592. # [19:38] <bent> where it verifies your QI implementation
  2593. # [19:38] * Joins: bnicholson (bnicholson@moz-BBE3ABD.mv.mozilla.com)
  2594. # [19:39] <bent> that's really all the magic there is
  2595. # [19:39] * Quits: Optimizer (Optimizer@82349606.9B33ED22.BE90E62C.IP) (Ping timeout)
  2596. # [19:39] <bent> so, for 1) above, Mook_as is right, if nsCOMPtr can't implicitly cast your T* to nsISupports then it can't verify QI
  2597. # [19:40] <bent> (and it won't be able to if T multiply-inherits nsISupports)
  2598. # [19:40] <bent> and 2) is right also, since you can't call a function that doesn't exist on T with a T*

  2611. # [19:43] <bent> this is the problem with nsCOMPtr<Foo>:
  2612. # [19:43] <bent> say you do this:
  2613. # [19:43] <bent> nsCOMPtr<Foo> foo = new Foo();
  2614. # [19:43] * Joins: Optimizer (Optimizer@1F4532D9.4F84BE42.BE90E62C.IP)
  2615. # [19:44] <bent> under the hood that will do |operator=(Foo* aRHS) { Foo* tmp; CallQueryInterface(tmp, aRHS); }|
  2616. # [19:44] <bent> i'm simplifying a bit
  2617. # [19:45] * Joins: marco (Thunderbir@A49E7235.B1299530.10DC0B64.IP)
  2618. # [19:45] <bent> so CallQueryInterface will try to figure out which IID to QI to
  2619. # [19:45] <bent> now, Foo shouldn't have an IID
  2620. # [19:45] <bent> nsIFoo, sure
  2621. # [19:45] <bent> but not Foo
  2622. # [19:45] <bent> nevertheless, due to the way we implement our IID helpers,
  2623. # [19:46] <bent> QI will see the IID of nsIFoo on Foo and use that
  2624. # [19:46] <bent> (probably)
  2625. # [19:46] <bent> there's a bug to make that fail, at which point nsCOMPtr<Foo> would no longer compile
  2626. # [19:46] <bent> but so far we haven't fixed it
  2627. # [19:47] * Quits: pascalc (chatzilla@moz-446F98C8.fbxo.proxad.net) (Ping timeout)
  2628. # [19:47] <bent> anyway, that means that the pointer QueryInterface will return is an nsIFoo*
  2629. # [19:47] <bent> not a Foo*
  2630. # [19:47] <bent> in most cases they will be the same
  2631. # [19:47] <bent> but not in all cases
